 This means that the way you watch your TV can change
 philhal ye saaf nahin he ki nae badlaavon se pareshaani badhegi yaa pehle se behatar anubhav milegaa
 TRAI says that new rules are being introduced for good changes
 jo bhi nae niyam aa rahe hai unamem se ek aisa bhi niyam hoga ki graahak bazaar se apana khud kaa set-top box (STB) kharid sakate hai
 In such a situation, you will not be obliged to use STB provided by companies providing DTH service such as Airtel, dishtv, tatasky
 TRAI kaa kahana he ki DTH sarvice prowiders yaa local cabel operators ab graahakon ko unase STB kharidne yaa kiraye par lene ke liye baadhya nahin kar sakate
 Now customers can purchase stbs from companies providing DTH service on rent or from the open market of their own choice
 yani aasaan bhashaa main kahen to ye kuch vaisaa hi he jaise aap broadband lene ke baad apni marji se router or modem kharid sakate hai yaa sarvice prowider se bhi le sakate hai
 According to the new rule, you can take STB from anywhere but it should be compatible for TV channels of the distributor
 nae niyam aane ke baad se ek technology ko standard banaaya jayega

 haalanki aisa niyam ab lagu nahin kiya gaya tha kyonki bazaar main maujuud stbs main alag tarah kii compresssont takanic, koding takanic, inkripshan system, middleware or oparating system hota he jo har STB ko unic banaata he
